    (function(i,s,o,g,r,a,m){i['GoogleAnalyticsObject']=r;i[r]=i[r]||function(){
 		(i[r].q=i[r].q||[]).push(arguments)},i[r].l=1*new Date();a=s.createElement(o),
 		m=s.getElementsByTagName(o)[0];a.async=1;a.src=g;m.parentNode.insertBefore(a,m)
 	})(window,document,'script','//www.google-analytics.com/analytics.js','ga');
 
 	
 		ga('create', 'UA-1300352-2', 'auto');

 	ga('require', 'ecommerce'); //load ecommerce plugin

 	$(function() {
 		
 		$(".ga-click-tracking").on("click", function(e){
 			var eventCategory="unknown",eventAction="unknown",eventLabel="unknown",eventValue="unknown";
 			if ($(this).hasClass("ga-click-tracking")) {
 				eventAction = 'click';
 			}
 			eventCategory = $(this).data("ga-category");
 			eventLabel = $(this).data("ga-label");
 			eventValue = $(this).data("ga-value");
 			sendEventToGA(eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue);
 		});
 		$(".link-element[data-href]").on("click",function(e){
 			e.stopPropagation();
 			if ($(this).data("href") !== undefined) {
 				if ($(this).data("event-name") !== undefined && $(this).data("event-category") !== undefined) {
 					sendEventToGA($(this).data('event-category'),'click',$(this).data('event-name'),1);
 				}
 				window.location.href=$(this).data("href");
 			}
 		});
 	});
 
 	function sendEventToGA(eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue) {
 		if (eventValue===undefined) {
 			eventValue=1;
 		};
 		
 		ga('send','event',eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue);
 	};

    var cartItemCount = null;
 var addToCartAnimsCount = 0;
 var ShoppingCartSummaryContent = null;
 $(document).ready(function() {
 	$("#QuickShopFlyoutItem").on("click", function() {
 		quickshopDialog();
 	});
 	$("#AccountFlyoutItem").on("mouseenter click", function() {
 		ManageMenuFlyout('AccountFlyout','/index.cfm?fuseaction=Account.displayAccountFlyout');
 	});
 	$("body").delegate(".linkLogin", "click", loginDialog);
 	
 	
 		/*
 		$("#EmailSignUpFooterForm").on("submit", function() {
 			ManageMenuFlyout('EmailFlyout','/index.cfm?fuseaction=Contact.displayEmailFlyout');
 			return false;
 		});
 		*/
 	
 
 	//MobileNavigation();
 	
 		$('#SearchText').sayt({
 			subdomain: 'threebscientific',
 			collection: 'DEDE',
 			defaultImage: '',
 			area: 'GermanyGerman',
 			selectSearchTerm: function (data) {
 				$('#SearchText').val(data.value);
 				$('#SearchOrigin').val('sayt');
 				$('#SearchForm').submit();
 			},
 	        selectProduct: function (data) {
 				window.location.href = data.url;
 	        }
 	        ,
 	        autocompleteTemplate: 'at',
 	        productTemplate: 'pt_DEDE',
 	        fuzzyMatch: true,
 	        numNavigations: 0,
 	        numProducts: 5,
 	        language: 'lang_de',
 	        onRenderProductsFinished: function(ul) {
 				var images = ul.find('img[src=""]').attr("src", "/_images/ProductImageComingSoon/50DE.gif");
 				if (ul.attr('id') != 'sayt-menu') {
 					ul.attr('id', 'sayt-menu');
 				}
 			}
 		});
 		$("#SearchForm").on("submit",function(e){
 			e.preventDefault();
 			window.location.href = getSearchURL($(this).find('[name=SearchText]').val(),$(this).find('#SearchOrigin').val());
 		});
 
 	
 		$(".headerCart").popover({
 			trigger: 'manual',
 			html: true,
 			title: '<a href="https://www.3bscientific.de/cart.html">In Ihrem Warenkorb</a>',
 			content: function() {
 				return ShoppingCartSummaryContent;
 			},
 			placement: 'bottom'
 		});
 		$(".headerCart").on("mouseenter",function (e){
 			e.preventDefault();
 			e.stopPropagation();
 			if (ShoppingCartSummaryContent != null) {
 				$(".headerCart").popover('show');
 				
 					if (typeof viewShoppingCartSummaryEvent == 'function') {
 						viewShoppingCartSummaryEvent();
 					}
 				
 				var PopoverTop = parseInt($(".headerCart").next("div.popover:visible").css("top"));
 				$(".headerCart").next("div.popover:visible").css("top",(PopoverTop + 15).toString() + "px" );
 				$("#ShoppingCartSummary").closest(".popover").on("mouseleave", function(e){
 					e.preventDefault();
 					e.stopPropagation();
 					$("#ShoppingCartSummary").closest(".popover").unbind("mouseleave");
 					$(".headerCart").popover('hide');
 				});
 			} else {
 				$.post(
 					"/index.cfm?fuseaction=Cart.displayCartSummary"
 				).done( function (data){
 					ShoppingCartSummaryContent = data;
 					$(".headerCart").trigger('mouseenter');
 				});
 			}
 		});
 	
 	
 	$('.add-to-cart').on('click', function (e) {
 		e.preventDefault();
 		e.stopPropagation();
 		cartItemCount = null;
 		var imgtodrag = null;
 		ShoppingCartSummaryContent = null;
 		// submit the form as first in the background
 		$(this).closest('.AddProductToCartForm').submit();
 		// find the image to drag into the shopping cart
 		
 		if (imgtodrag == null || imgtodrag.length == 0) {
 			if ($('#ProductImageContainer').length > 0) {
 				imgtodrag = $('#ProductImageContainer').find("#ZoomerOuter").eq(0).find("img").eq(0);
 				if (imgtodrag.length === 0) {
 					imgtodrag = $('#ProductImageContainer').find("img");
 				}
 			} else {
 				var productID = $(this).closest('.AddProductToCartForm').find('[name=ProductID]').val();
 				imgtodrag = $('#productImage' + productID);
 			}
 		}
 		$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 'fast');
 
 		var cart = $('.shopping-cart');
 		if (imgtodrag.length > 0 && cart.length > 0) {
 			addToCartAnimsCount += 1;
 			var imgclone = imgtodrag.clone()
 				.offset({
 					top: imgtodrag.offset().top,
 					left: imgtodrag.offset().left
 				})
 				.css({
 					'opacity': '0.5',
 					'position': 'absolute',
 					'z-index': '100'
 	            })
 					.appendTo($('body'))
 					.animate({
 					'top': cart.offset().top + 10,
 					'left': cart.offset().left + 10,
 					'width': 75,
 					'height': 75
 	            }, 1500, 'easeInOutExpo');
 			imgclone.animate({
 					'width': 0,
 					'height': 0
 			}, function () {
 				$(this).detach();
 				addToCartAnimsCount -= 1;
 				if (cartItemCount != null && addToCartAnimsCount < 1) {
 					$(".CartItemCount").html(cartItemCount);
 					cartItemCount = null;
 				}
 			});
 		}
 	});
 
 });
 
 
 function loginDialog(displayMessage)
 {
 	var displayMessageParam = '';
 	if (displayMessage !== undefined) {
 		displayMessageParam = '&displayMessage=' + displayMessage;
 	}
 	$.post(
 		"https://www.3bscientific.de/index.cfm?fuseaction=Account.displayLoginPopup" + displayMessageParam
 	).done(function( data ) {
 		$('#LoginModalContainer .modal-body').html(data);
 		$('#LoginModalContainer .modal-footer #FormSubmit').show();
 		$('#LoginFormModal').modal('show');
 	});
 	return false;
 }
 
 function quickshopDialog()
 {
 	$.post(
 		"/index.cfm?fuseaction=Cart.displayQuickShop"
 	).done(function( data ) {
 		$('#QuickshopModalContainer .modal-body').html(data);
 		$('#QuickModalContainer .modal-footer #FormSubmit').show();
 		$('#QuickshopFormModal').modal('show');
 	});
 	return false;
 }
 
 
 	function getSearchURL(SearchText, SearchOrigin) {
 		var url = '/';
 		if (SearchText.length === 0) {
 			SearchText = ' ';
 		}
 		var SearchTextCleaned = SearchText.replace(/\//g,'--');
 		url += SearchTextCleaned.replace(/ /g,'+') + '/q/?SearchText=' + encodeURIComponent(SearchText);
 		if (SearchOrigin.length > 0) {
 			url += '&SearchOrigin=' + SearchOrigin;
 		}
 		return url;
 	}

 	TwitterStylesTries--;

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var gbTracker = null;
 	$(document).ready(function() {
 		gbTracker = initializeGbTracker(gbTracker);
 	});
 
 	function sendGbTrackerEvent(eventName,params) {
 		gbTracker = initializeGbTracker(gbTracker);
 		switch(eventName) {
 			case 'search':
 				sendGbTrackerSearchEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'addToCart':
 				sendGbTrackerAddToCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'viewCart':
 				sendGbTrackerViewCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'removeFromCart':
 				sendGbTrackerRemoveFromCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'viewProduct':
 				sendGbTrackerViewProductEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'order':
 				sendGbTrackerOrderEvent(params);
 				break;
 		    default:
 				alert('unknown event');
 		}
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerSearchEvent(params) {
 		var searchEvent = {
 			search: {
 				id: params.id,
 				origin: {
 					recommendations: false,
 					navigation:      false,
 					dym:             false,
 					sayt:            false,
 					search:          false
 				}
 			}
 		};
 		searchEvent.search.origin[params.origin] = true;
 		if ('metadata' in params) {
 			searchEvent['metadata'] = params.metadata;
 		}
 		gbTracker.sendAutoSearchEvent(searchEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerAddToCartEvent(params) {
 		var addToCartEvent = {
 			cart: params
 		};
 		//console.log(addToCartEvent);
 		gbTracker.sendAddToCartEvent(addToCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerViewCartEvent(params) {
 		var viewCartEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.CartID,
 				items: params.Items
 			}
 		};
 //		console.log(viewCartEvent);
 		gbTracker.sendViewCartEvent(viewCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerRemoveFromCartEvent(params) {
 		var removeFromCartEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.CartID,
 				items: params.Items
 			}
 		};
 //		console.log(removeFromCartEvent);
 //		return;
 		gbTracker.sendRemoveFromCartEvent(removeFromCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerViewProductEvent(params) {
 		var viewProductEvent = {
 			product: params.product
 		};
 //		console.log(viewProductEvent);
 //		return;
 		gbTracker.sendViewProductEvent(viewProductEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerOrderEvent(params) {
 		var orderEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.cartId,
 				totalItems: params.totalItems,
 				totalQuantity: params.totalQuantity,
 				totalPrice: params.totalPrice,
 				items: params.items
 			}
 		};
 		gbTracker.sendOrderEvent(orderEvent);
 	}
 
 
 	// initialise the gbTracker if not initialiased yet
 	function initializeGbTracker(gbTrackerObject) {
 		if (gbTrackerObject !== null) {
 			return gbTrackerObject;
 		}
 		var gbTrackerLocal = new GbTracker('threebscientific', 'GermanyGerman');
 		
 			gbTrackerLocal.autoSetVisitor();
 		
 		return gbTrackerLocal;
 	}
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    (function(i,s,o,g,r,a,m){i['GoogleAnalyticsObject']=r;i[r]=i[r]||function(){
 		(i[r].q=i[r].q||[]).push(arguments)},i[r].l=1*new Date();a=s.createElement(o),
 		m=s.getElementsByTagName(o)[0];a.async=1;a.src=g;m.parentNode.insertBefore(a,m)
 	})(window,document,'script','//www.google-analytics.com/analytics.js','ga');
 
 	
 		ga('create', 'UA-1300352-2', 'auto');
 	
 	ga('require', 'displayfeatures');
 	ga('require', 'ecommerce'); //load ecommerce plugin
 	
 		ga('set', 'anonymizeIp', true);
 	
 	ga('send', 'pageview');
 
 	
 
 	$(function() {
 		
 		$(".ga-click-tracking").on("click", function(e){
 			var eventCategory="unknown",eventAction="unknown",eventLabel="unknown",eventValue="unknown";
 			if ($(this).hasClass("ga-click-tracking")) {
 				eventAction = 'click';
 			}
 			eventCategory = $(this).data("ga-category");
 			eventLabel = $(this).data("ga-label");
 			eventValue = $(this).data("ga-value");
 			sendEventToGA(eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue);
 		});
 		$(".link-element[data-href]").on("click",function(e){
 			e.stopPropagation();
 			if ($(this).data("href") !== undefined) {
 				if ($(this).data("event-name") !== undefined && $(this).data("event-category") !== undefined) {
 					sendEventToGA($(this).data('event-category'),'click',$(this).data('event-name'),1);
 				}
 				window.location.href=$(this).data("href");
 			}
 		});
 	});
 
 	function sendEventToGA(eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue) {
 		if (eventValue===undefined) {
 			eventValue=1;
 		};
 		
 		ga('send','event',eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue);
 	};
   </script>

   <script>
    var cartItemCount = null;
 var addToCartAnimsCount = 0;
 var ShoppingCartSummaryContent = null;
 $(document).ready(function() {
 	$("#QuickShopFlyoutItem").on("click", function() {
 		quickshopDialog();
 	});
 	$("#AccountFlyoutItem").on("mouseenter click", function() {
 		ManageMenuFlyout('AccountFlyout','/index.cfm?fuseaction=Account.displayAccountFlyout');
 	});
 	$("body").delegate(".linkLogin", "click", loginDialog);
 	
 	
 		/*
 		$("#EmailSignUpFooterForm").on("submit", function() {
 			ManageMenuFlyout('EmailFlyout','/index.cfm?fuseaction=Contact.displayEmailFlyout');
 			return false;
 		});
 		*/
 	
 
 	//MobileNavigation();
 	
 		$('#SearchText').sayt({
 			subdomain: 'threebscientific',
 			collection: 'DEDE',
 			defaultImage: '',
 			area: 'GermanyGerman',
 			selectSearchTerm: function (data) {
 				$('#SearchText').val(data.value);
 				$('#SearchOrigin').val('sayt');
 				$('#SearchForm').submit();
 			},
 	        selectProduct: function (data) {
 				window.location.href = data.url;
 	        }
 	        ,
 	        autocompleteTemplate: 'at',
 	        productTemplate: 'pt_DEDE',
 	        fuzzyMatch: true,
 	        numNavigations: 0,
 	        numProducts: 5,
 	        language: 'lang_de',
 	        onRenderProductsFinished: function(ul) {
 				var images = ul.find('img[src=""]').attr("src", "/_images/ProductImageComingSoon/50DE.gif");
 				if (ul.attr('id') != 'sayt-menu') {
 					ul.attr('id', 'sayt-menu');
 				}
 			}
 		});
 		$("#SearchForm").on("submit",function(e){
 			e.preventDefault();
 			window.location.href = getSearchURL($(this).find('[name=SearchText]').val(),$(this).find('#SearchOrigin').val());
 		});
 
 	
 		$(".headerCart").popover({
 			trigger: 'manual',
 			html: true,
 			title: '<a href="https://www.3bscientific.de/cart.html">In Ihrem Warenkorb</a>',
 			content: function() {
 				return ShoppingCartSummaryContent;
 			},
 			placement: 'bottom'
 		});
 		$(".headerCart").on("mouseenter",function (e){
 			e.preventDefault();
 			e.stopPropagation();
 			if (ShoppingCartSummaryContent != null) {
 				$(".headerCart").popover('show');
 				
 					if (typeof viewShoppingCartSummaryEvent == 'function') {
 						viewShoppingCartSummaryEvent();
 					}
 				
 				var PopoverTop = parseInt($(".headerCart").next("div.popover:visible").css("top"));
 				$(".headerCart").next("div.popover:visible").css("top",(PopoverTop + 15).toString() + "px" );
 				$("#ShoppingCartSummary").closest(".popover").on("mouseleave", function(e){
 					e.preventDefault();
 					e.stopPropagation();
 					$("#ShoppingCartSummary").closest(".popover").unbind("mouseleave");
 					$(".headerCart").popover('hide');
 				});
 			} else {
 				$.post(
 					"/index.cfm?fuseaction=Cart.displayCartSummary"
 				).done( function (data){
 					ShoppingCartSummaryContent = data;
 					$(".headerCart").trigger('mouseenter');
 				});
 			}
 		});
 	
 	
 	$('.add-to-cart').on('click', function (e) {
 		e.preventDefault();
 		e.stopPropagation();
 		cartItemCount = null;
 		var imgtodrag = null;
 		ShoppingCartSummaryContent = null;
 		// submit the form as first in the background
 		$(this).closest('.AddProductToCartForm').submit();
 		// find the image to drag into the shopping cart
 		
 		if (imgtodrag == null || imgtodrag.length == 0) {
 			if ($('#ProductImageContainer').length > 0) {
 				imgtodrag = $('#ProductImageContainer').find("#ZoomerOuter").eq(0).find("img").eq(0);
 				if (imgtodrag.length === 0) {
 					imgtodrag = $('#ProductImageContainer').find("img");
 				}
 			} else {
 				var productID = $(this).closest('.AddProductToCartForm').find('[name=ProductID]').val();
 				imgtodrag = $('#productImage' + productID);
 			}
 		}
 		$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 'fast');
 
 		var cart = $('.shopping-cart');
 		if (imgtodrag.length > 0 && cart.length > 0) {
 			addToCartAnimsCount += 1;
 			var imgclone = imgtodrag.clone()
 				.offset({
 					top: imgtodrag.offset().top,
 					left: imgtodrag.offset().left
 				})
 				.css({
 					'opacity': '0.5',
 					'position': 'absolute',
 					'z-index': '100'
 	            })
 					.appendTo($('body'))
 					.animate({
 					'top': cart.offset().top + 10,
 					'left': cart.offset().left + 10,
 					'width': 75,
 					'height': 75
 	            }, 1500, 'easeInOutExpo');
 			imgclone.animate({
 					'width': 0,
 					'height': 0
 			}, function () {
 				$(this).detach();
 				addToCartAnimsCount -= 1;
 				if (cartItemCount != null && addToCartAnimsCount < 1) {
 					$(".CartItemCount").html(cartItemCount);
 					cartItemCount = null;
 				}
 			});
 		}
 	});
 
 });
 
 
 function loginDialog(displayMessage)
 {
 	var displayMessageParam = '';
 	if (displayMessage !== undefined) {
 		displayMessageParam = '&displayMessage=' + displayMessage;
 	}
 	$.post(
 		"https://www.3bscientific.de/index.cfm?fuseaction=Account.displayLoginPopup" + displayMessageParam
 	).done(function( data ) {
 		$('#LoginModalContainer .modal-body').html(data);
 		$('#LoginModalContainer .modal-footer #FormSubmit').show();
 		$('#LoginFormModal').modal('show');
 	});
 	return false;
 }
 
 function quickshopDialog()
 {
 	$.post(
 		"/index.cfm?fuseaction=Cart.displayQuickShop"
 	).done(function( data ) {
 		$('#QuickshopModalContainer .modal-body').html(data);
 		$('#QuickModalContainer .modal-footer #FormSubmit').show();
 		$('#QuickshopFormModal').modal('show');
 	});
 	return false;
 }
 
 
 	function getSearchURL(SearchText, SearchOrigin) {
 		var url = '/';
 		if (SearchText.length === 0) {
 			SearchText = ' ';
 		}
 		var SearchTextCleaned = SearchText.replace(/\//g,'--');
 		url += SearchTextCleaned.replace(/ /g,'+') + '/q/?SearchText=' + encodeURIComponent(SearchText);
 		if (SearchOrigin.length > 0) {
 			url += '&SearchOrigin=' + SearchOrigin;
 		}
 		return url;
 	}

    var TwitterStylesIntervalID;
 var TwitterStylesTries = 10;
 
 function setTwitterStyles() {
 	if ($("iframe#twitter-widget-0").contents().find('head').length > 0 || TwitterStylesTries < 1) {
 		$("iframe#twitter-widget-0").contents().find('head').append('<style>img.u-photo,img.avatar{display:none;}body{color:#58595b;font-family:"proxima-nova",sans-serif;}.header{padding-left:0!important;min-height:20px!important;}span.full-name{float:left;}span.p-name{color:#4a96fe!important;font-size:140%!important;font-weight:400!important;margin-right:5px;}span.p-nickname{color:#959595;}p.e-entry-title{font-size:14px!important;line-height:1.25em!important;}.tweet{padding-left:0!important}</style>');
 		clearInterval(TwitterStylesIntervalID);
 		return;
 	}
 	TwitterStylesTries--;
 }

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var gbTracker = null;
 	$(document).ready(function() {
 		gbTracker = initializeGbTracker(gbTracker);
 	});
 
 	function sendGbTrackerEvent(eventName,params) {
 		gbTracker = initializeGbTracker(gbTracker);
 		switch(eventName) {
 			case 'search':
 				sendGbTrackerSearchEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'addToCart':
 				sendGbTrackerAddToCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'viewCart':
 				sendGbTrackerViewCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'removeFromCart':
 				sendGbTrackerRemoveFromCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'viewProduct':
 				sendGbTrackerViewProductEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'order':
 				sendGbTrackerOrderEvent(params);
 				break;
 		    default:
 				alert('unknown event');
 		}
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerSearchEvent(params) {
 		var searchEvent = {
 			search: {
 				id: params.id,
 				origin: {
 					recommendations: false,
 					navigation:      false,
 					dym:             false,
 					sayt:            false,
 					search:          false
 				}
 			}
 		};
 		searchEvent.search.origin[params.origin] = true;
 		if ('metadata' in params) {
 			searchEvent['metadata'] = params.metadata;
 		}
 		gbTracker.sendAutoSearchEvent(searchEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerAddToCartEvent(params) {
 		var addToCartEvent = {
 			cart: params
 		};
 		//console.log(addToCartEvent);
 		gbTracker.sendAddToCartEvent(addToCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerViewCartEvent(params) {
 		var viewCartEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.CartID,
 				items: params.Items
 			}
 		};
 //		console.log(viewCartEvent);
 		gbTracker.sendViewCartEvent(viewCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerRemoveFromCartEvent(params) {
 		var removeFromCartEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.CartID,
 				items: params.Items
 			}
 		};
 //		console.log(removeFromCartEvent);
 //		return;
 		gbTracker.sendRemoveFromCartEvent(removeFromCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerViewProductEvent(params) {
 		var viewProductEvent = {
 			product: params.product
 		};
 //		console.log(viewProductEvent);
 //		return;
 		gbTracker.sendViewProductEvent(viewProductEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerOrderEvent(params) {
 		var orderEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.cartId,
 				totalItems: params.totalItems,
 				totalQuantity: params.totalQuantity,
 				totalPrice: params.totalPrice,
 				items: params.items
 			}
 		};
 		gbTracker.sendOrderEvent(orderEvent);
 	}
 
 
 	// initialise the gbTracker if not initialiased yet
 	function initializeGbTracker(gbTrackerObject) {
 		if (gbTrackerObject !== null) {
 			return gbTrackerObject;
 		}
 		var gbTrackerLocal = new GbTracker('threebscientific', 'GermanyGerman');
 		
 			gbTrackerLocal.autoSetVisitor();
 		
 		return gbTrackerLocal;
 	}
   </script>

 	$(function() {
 		
 		$(".ga-click-tracking").on("click", function(e){
 			var eventCategory="unknown",eventAction="unknown",eventLabel="unknown",eventValue="unknown";
 			if ($(this).hasClass("ga-click-tracking")) {
 				eventAction = 'click';
 			}
 			eventCategory = $(this).data("ga-category");
 			eventLabel = $(this).data("ga-label");
 			eventValue = $(this).data("ga-value");
 			sendEventToGA(eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue);
 		});
 		$(".link-element[data-href]").on("click",function(e){
 			e.stopPropagation();
 			if ($(this).data("href") !== undefined) {
 				if ($(this).data("event-name") !== undefined && $(this).data("event-category") !== undefined) {
 					sendEventToGA($(this).data('event-category'),'click',$(this).data('event-name'),1);
 				}
 				window.location.href=$(this).data("href");
 			}
 		});
 	});
 
 	function sendEventToGA(eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue) {
 		if (eventValue===undefined) {
 			eventValue=1;
 		};
 		
 		ga('send','event',eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue);
 	};

 		$('#SearchText').sayt({
 			subdomain: 'threebscientific',
 			collection: 'DEDE',
 			defaultImage: '',
 			area: 'GermanyGerman',
 			selectSearchTerm: function (data) {
 				$('#SearchText').val(data.value);
 				$('#SearchOrigin').val('sayt');
 				$('#SearchForm').submit();
 			},
 	        selectProduct: function (data) {
 				window.location.href = data.url;
 	        }
 	        ,
 	        autocompleteTemplate: 'at',
 	        productTemplate: 'pt_DEDE',
 	        fuzzyMatch: true,
 	        numNavigations: 0,
 	        numProducts: 5,
 	        language: 'lang_de',
 	        onRenderProductsFinished: function(ul) {
 				var images = ul.find('img[src=""]').attr("src", "/_images/ProductImageComingSoon/50DE.gif");
 				if (ul.attr('id') != 'sayt-menu') {
 					ul.attr('id', 'sayt-menu');
 				}
 			}
 		});
 		$("#SearchForm").on("submit",function(e){
 			e.preventDefault();
 			window.location.href = getSearchURL($(this).find('[name=SearchText]').val(),$(this).find('#SearchOrigin').val());
 		});
 
 	
 		$(".headerCart").popover({
 			trigger: 'manual',
 			html: true,
 			title: '<a href="https://www.3bscientific.de/cart.html">In Ihrem Warenkorb</a>',
 			content: function() {
 				return ShoppingCartSummaryContent;
 			},
 			placement: 'bottom'
 		});
 		$(".headerCart").on("mouseenter",function (e){
 			e.preventDefault();
 			e.stopPropagation();
 			if (ShoppingCartSummaryContent != null) {
 				$(".headerCart").popover('show');
 				
 					if (typeof viewShoppingCartSummaryEvent == 'function') {
 						viewShoppingCartSummaryEvent();
 					}
 				
 				var PopoverTop = parseInt($(".headerCart").next("div.popover:visible").css("top"));
 				$(".headerCart").next("div.popover:visible").css("top",(PopoverTop + 15).toString() + "px" );
 				$("#ShoppingCartSummary").closest(".popover").on("mouseleave", function(e){
 					e.preventDefault();
 					e.stopPropagation();
 					$("#ShoppingCartSummary").closest(".popover").unbind("mouseleave");
 					$(".headerCart").popover('hide');
 				});
 			} else {
 				$.post(
 					"/index.cfm?fuseaction=Cart.displayCartSummary"
 				).done( function (data){
 					ShoppingCartSummaryContent = data;
 					$(".headerCart").trigger('mouseenter');
 				});
 			}
 		});
 	
 	
 	$('.add-to-cart').on('click', function (e) {
 		e.preventDefault();
 		e.stopPropagation();
 		cartItemCount = null;
 		var imgtodrag = null;
 		ShoppingCartSummaryContent = null;
 		// submit the form as first in the background
 		$(this).closest('.AddProductToCartForm').submit();
 		// find the image to drag into the shopping cart
 		
 		if (imgtodrag == null || imgtodrag.length == 0) {
 			if ($('#ProductImageContainer').length > 0) {
 				imgtodrag = $('#ProductImageContainer').find("#ZoomerOuter").eq(0).find("img").eq(0);
 				if (imgtodrag.length === 0) {
 					imgtodrag = $('#ProductImageContainer').find("img");
 				}
 			} else {
 				var productID = $(this).closest('.AddProductToCartForm').find('[name=ProductID]').val();
 				imgtodrag = $('#productImage' + productID);
 			}
 		}
 		$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 'fast');
 
 		var cart = $('.shopping-cart');
 		if (imgtodrag.length > 0 && cart.length > 0) {
 			addToCartAnimsCount += 1;
 			var imgclone = imgtodrag.clone()
 				.offset({
 					top: imgtodrag.offset().top,
 					left: imgtodrag.offset().left
 				})
 				.css({
 					'opacity': '0.5',
 					'position': 'absolute',
 					'z-index': '100'
 	            })
 					.appendTo($('body'))
 					.animate({
 					'top': cart.offset().top + 10,
 					'left': cart.offset().left + 10,
 					'width': 75,
 					'height': 75
 	            }, 1500, 'easeInOutExpo');
 			imgclone.animate({
 					'width': 0,
 					'height': 0
 			}, function () {
 				$(this).detach();
 				addToCartAnimsCount -= 1;
 				if (cartItemCount != null && addToCartAnimsCount < 1) {
 					$(".CartItemCount").html(cartItemCount);
 					cartItemCount = null;
 				}
 			});
 		}
 	});
 
 });
 
 
 function loginDialog(displayMessage)
 {
 	var displayMessageParam = '';
 	if (displayMessage !== undefined) {
 		displayMessageParam = '&displayMessage=' + displayMessage;
 	}
 	$.post(
 		"https://www.3bscientific.de/index.cfm?fuseaction=Account.displayLoginPopup" + displayMessageParam
 	).done(function( data ) {
 		$('#LoginModalContainer .modal-body').html(data);
 		$('#LoginModalContainer .modal-footer #FormSubmit').show();
 		$('#LoginFormModal').modal('show');
 	});
 	return false;
 }
 
 function quickshopDialog()
 {
 	$.post(
 		"/index.cfm?fuseaction=Cart.displayQuickShop"
 	).done(function( data ) {
 		$('#QuickshopModalContainer .modal-body').html(data);
 		$('#QuickModalContainer .modal-footer #FormSubmit').show();
 		$('#QuickshopFormModal').modal('show');
 	});
 	return false;
 }
 
 
 	function getSearchURL(SearchText, SearchOrigin) {
 		var url = '/';
 		if (SearchText.length === 0) {
 			SearchText = ' ';
 		}
 		var SearchTextCleaned = SearchText.replace(/\//g,'--');
 		url += SearchTextCleaned.replace(/ /g,'+') + '/q/?SearchText=' + encodeURIComponent(SearchText);
 		if (SearchOrigin.length > 0) {
 			url += '&SearchOrigin=' + SearchOrigin;
 		}
 		return url;
 	}

 var TwitterStylesTries = 10;
 
 function setTwitterStyles() {
 	if ($("iframe#twitter-widget-0").contents().find('head').length > 0 || TwitterStylesTries < 1) {
 		$("iframe#twitter-widget-0").contents().find('head').append('<style>img.u-photo,img.avatar{display:none;}body{color:#58595b;font-family:"proxima-nova",sans-serif;}.header{padding-left:0!important;min-height:20px!important;}span.full-name{float:left;}span.p-name{color:#4a96fe!important;font-size:140%!important;font-weight:400!important;margin-right:5px;}span.p-nickname{color:#959595;}p.e-entry-title{font-size:14px!important;line-height:1.25em!important;}.tweet{padding-left:0!important}</style>');
 		clearInterval(TwitterStylesIntervalID);
 		return;
 	}
 	TwitterStylesTries--;
 }

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var gbTracker = null;
 	$(document).ready(function() {
 		gbTracker = initializeGbTracker(gbTracker);
 	});
 
 	function sendGbTrackerEvent(eventName,params) {
 		gbTracker = initializeGbTracker(gbTracker);
 		switch(eventName) {
 			case 'search':
 				sendGbTrackerSearchEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'addToCart':
 				sendGbTrackerAddToCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'viewCart':
 				sendGbTrackerViewCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'removeFromCart':
 				sendGbTrackerRemoveFromCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'viewProduct':
 				sendGbTrackerViewProductEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'order':
 				sendGbTrackerOrderEvent(params);
 				break;
 		    default:
 				alert('unknown event');
 		}
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerSearchEvent(params) {
 		var searchEvent = {
 			search: {
 				id: params.id,
 				origin: {
 					recommendations: false,
 					navigation:      false,
 					dym:             false,
 					sayt:            false,
 					search:          false
 				}
 			}
 		};
 		searchEvent.search.origin[params.origin] = true;
 		if ('metadata' in params) {
 			searchEvent['metadata'] = params.metadata;
 		}
 		gbTracker.sendAutoSearchEvent(searchEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerAddToCartEvent(params) {
 		var addToCartEvent = {
 			cart: params
 		};
 		//console.log(addToCartEvent);
 		gbTracker.sendAddToCartEvent(addToCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerViewCartEvent(params) {
 		var viewCartEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.CartID,
 				items: params.Items
 			}
 		};
 //		console.log(viewCartEvent);
 		gbTracker.sendViewCartEvent(viewCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerRemoveFromCartEvent(params) {
 		var removeFromCartEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.CartID,
 				items: params.Items
 			}
 		};
 //		console.log(removeFromCartEvent);
 //		return;
 		gbTracker.sendRemoveFromCartEvent(removeFromCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerViewProductEvent(params) {
 		var viewProductEvent = {
 			product: params.product
 		};
 //		console.log(viewProductEvent);
 //		return;
 		gbTracker.sendViewProductEvent(viewProductEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerOrderEvent(params) {
 		var orderEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.cartId,
 				totalItems: params.totalItems,
 				totalQuantity: params.totalQuantity,
 				totalPrice: params.totalPrice,
 				items: params.items
 			}
 		};
 		gbTracker.sendOrderEvent(orderEvent);
 	}
 
 
 	// initialise the gbTracker if not initialiased yet
 	function initializeGbTracker(gbTrackerObject) {
 		if (gbTrackerObject !== null) {
 			return gbTrackerObject;
 		}
 		var gbTrackerLocal = new GbTracker('threebscientific', 'GermanyGerman');
 		
 			gbTrackerLocal.autoSetVisitor();
 		
 		return gbTrackerLocal;
 	}
   </script>

    (function(i,s,o,g,r,a,m){i['GoogleAnalyticsObject']=r;i[r]=i[r]||function(){

 	$(function() {
 		
 		$(".ga-click-tracking").on("click", function(e){
 			var eventCategory="unknown",eventAction="unknown",eventLabel="unknown",eventValue="unknown";
 			if ($(this).hasClass("ga-click-tracking")) {
 				eventAction = 'click';
 			}
 			eventCategory = $(this).data("ga-category");
 			eventLabel = $(this).data("ga-label");
 			eventValue = $(this).data("ga-value");
 			sendEventToGA(eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue);
 		});
 		$(".link-element[data-href]").on("click",function(e){
 			e.stopPropagation();
 			if ($(this).data("href") !== undefined) {
 				if ($(this).data("event-name") !== undefined && $(this).data("event-category") !== undefined) {
 					sendEventToGA($(this).data('event-category'),'click',$(this).data('event-name'),1);
 				}
 				window.location.href=$(this).data("href");
 			}
 		});
 	});
 
 	function sendEventToGA(eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue) {
 		if (eventValue===undefined) {
 			eventValue=1;
 		};
 		
 		ga('send','event',eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue);
 	};

   <script>
    var cartItemCount = null;
 var addToCartAnimsCount = 0;
 var ShoppingCartSummaryContent = null;
 $(document).ready(function() {
 	$("#QuickShopFlyoutItem").on("click", function() {
 		quickshopDialog();
 	});

 	//MobileNavigation();
 	
 		$('#SearchText').sayt({
 			subdomain: 'threebscientific',
 			collection: 'DEDE',
 			defaultImage: '',
 			area: 'GermanyGerman',
 			selectSearchTerm: function (data) {
 				$('#SearchText').val(data.value);
 				$('#SearchOrigin').val('sayt');
 				$('#SearchForm').submit();
 			},
 	        selectProduct: function (data) {
 				window.location.href = data.url;
 	        }
 	        ,
 	        autocompleteTemplate: 'at',
 	        productTemplate: 'pt_DEDE',
 	        fuzzyMatch: true,
 	        numNavigations: 0,
 	        numProducts: 5,
 	        language: 'lang_de',
 	        onRenderProductsFinished: function(ul) {
 				var images = ul.find('img[src=""]').attr("src", "/_images/ProductImageComingSoon/50DE.gif");
 				if (ul.attr('id') != 'sayt-menu') {
 					ul.attr('id', 'sayt-menu');
 				}
 			}
 		});
 		$("#SearchForm").on("submit",function(e){
 			e.preventDefault();
 			window.location.href = getSearchURL($(this).find('[name=SearchText]').val(),$(this).find('#SearchOrigin').val());
 		});
 
 	
 		$(".headerCart").popover({
 			trigger: 'manual',
 			html: true,
 			title: '<a href="https://www.3bscientific.de/cart.html">In Ihrem Warenkorb</a>',
 			content: function() {
 				return ShoppingCartSummaryContent;
 			},
 			placement: 'bottom'
 		});
 		$(".headerCart").on("mouseenter",function (e){
 			e.preventDefault();
 			e.stopPropagation();
 			if (ShoppingCartSummaryContent != null) {
 				$(".headerCart").popover('show');
 				
 					if (typeof viewShoppingCartSummaryEvent == 'function') {
 						viewShoppingCartSummaryEvent();
 					}
 				
 				var PopoverTop = parseInt($(".headerCart").next("div.popover:visible").css("top"));
 				$(".headerCart").next("div.popover:visible").css("top",(PopoverTop + 15).toString() + "px" );
 				$("#ShoppingCartSummary").closest(".popover").on("mouseleave", function(e){
 					e.preventDefault();
 					e.stopPropagation();
 					$("#ShoppingCartSummary").closest(".popover").unbind("mouseleave");
 					$(".headerCart").popover('hide');
 				});
 			} else {
 				$.post(
 					"/index.cfm?fuseaction=Cart.displayCartSummary"
 				).done( function (data){
 					ShoppingCartSummaryContent = data;
 					$(".headerCart").trigger('mouseenter');
 				});
 			}
 		});
 	
 	
 	$('.add-to-cart').on('click', function (e) {
 		e.preventDefault();
 		e.stopPropagation();
 		cartItemCount = null;
 		var imgtodrag = null;
 		ShoppingCartSummaryContent = null;
 		// submit the form as first in the background
 		$(this).closest('.AddProductToCartForm').submit();
 		// find the image to drag into the shopping cart
 		
 		if (imgtodrag == null || imgtodrag.length == 0) {
 			if ($('#ProductImageContainer').length > 0) {
 				imgtodrag = $('#ProductImageContainer').find("#ZoomerOuter").eq(0).find("img").eq(0);
 				if (imgtodrag.length === 0) {
 					imgtodrag = $('#ProductImageContainer').find("img");
 				}
 			} else {
 				var productID = $(this).closest('.AddProductToCartForm').find('[name=ProductID]').val();
 				imgtodrag = $('#productImage' + productID);
 			}
 		}
 		$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 'fast');
 
 		var cart = $('.shopping-cart');
 		if (imgtodrag.length > 0 && cart.length > 0) {
 			addToCartAnimsCount += 1;
 			var imgclone = imgtodrag.clone()
 				.offset({
 					top: imgtodrag.offset().top,
 					left: imgtodrag.offset().left
 				})
 				.css({
 					'opacity': '0.5',
 					'position': 'absolute',
 					'z-index': '100'
 	            })
 					.appendTo($('body'))
 					.animate({
 					'top': cart.offset().top + 10,
 					'left': cart.offset().left + 10,
 					'width': 75,
 					'height': 75
 	            }, 1500, 'easeInOutExpo');
 			imgclone.animate({
 					'width': 0,
 					'height': 0
 			}, function () {
 				$(this).detach();
 				addToCartAnimsCount -= 1;
 				if (cartItemCount != null && addToCartAnimsCount < 1) {
 					$(".CartItemCount").html(cartItemCount);
 					cartItemCount = null;
 				}
 			});
 		}
 	});
 
 });
 
 
 function loginDialog(displayMessage)
 {
 	var displayMessageParam = '';
 	if (displayMessage !== undefined) {
 		displayMessageParam = '&displayMessage=' + displayMessage;
 	}
 	$.post(
 		"https://www.3bscientific.de/index.cfm?fuseaction=Account.displayLoginPopup" + displayMessageParam
 	).done(function( data ) {
 		$('#LoginModalContainer .modal-body').html(data);
 		$('#LoginModalContainer .modal-footer #FormSubmit').show();
 		$('#LoginFormModal').modal('show');
 	});
 	return false;
 }
 
 function quickshopDialog()
 {
 	$.post(
 		"/index.cfm?fuseaction=Cart.displayQuickShop"
 	).done(function( data ) {
 		$('#QuickshopModalContainer .modal-body').html(data);
 		$('#QuickModalContainer .modal-footer #FormSubmit').show();
 		$('#QuickshopFormModal').modal('show');
 	});
 	return false;
 }
 
 
 	function getSearchURL(SearchText, SearchOrigin) {
 		var url = '/';
 		if (SearchText.length === 0) {
 			SearchText = ' ';
 		}
 		var SearchTextCleaned = SearchText.replace(/\//g,'--');
 		url += SearchTextCleaned.replace(/ /g,'+') + '/q/?SearchText=' + encodeURIComponent(SearchText);
 		if (SearchOrigin.length > 0) {
 			url += '&SearchOrigin=' + SearchOrigin;
 		}
 		return url;
 	}
   </script>

    var TwitterStylesIntervalID;
 var TwitterStylesTries = 10;
 
 function setTwitterStyles() {
 	if ($("iframe#twitter-widget-0").contents().find('head').length > 0 || TwitterStylesTries < 1) {
 		$("iframe#twitter-widget-0").contents().find('head').append('<style>img.u-photo,img.avatar{display:none;}body{color:#58595b;font-family:"proxima-nova",sans-serif;}.header{padding-left:0!important;min-height:20px!important;}span.full-name{float:left;}span.p-name{color:#4a96fe!important;font-size:140%!important;font-weight:400!important;margin-right:5px;}span.p-nickname{color:#959595;}p.e-entry-title{font-size:14px!important;line-height:1.25em!important;}.tweet{padding-left:0!important}</style>');
 		clearInterval(TwitterStylesIntervalID);
 		return;
 	}
 	TwitterStylesTries--;
 }

 {

 	});

 });

   <script type="text/javascript">
    var gbTracker = null;
 	$(document).ready(function() {
 		gbTracker = initializeGbTracker(gbTracker);
 	});
 
 	function sendGbTrackerEvent(eventName,params) {
 		gbTracker = initializeGbTracker(gbTracker);
 		switch(eventName) {
 			case 'search':
 				sendGbTrackerSearchEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'addToCart':
 				sendGbTrackerAddToCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'viewCart':
 				sendGbTrackerViewCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'removeFromCart':
 				sendGbTrackerRemoveFromCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'viewProduct':
 				sendGbTrackerViewProductEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'order':
 				sendGbTrackerOrderEvent(params);
 				break;
 		    default:
 				alert('unknown event');
 		}
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerSearchEvent(params) {
 		var searchEvent = {
 			search: {
 				id: params.id,
 				origin: {
 					recommendations: false,
 					navigation:      false,
 					dym:             false,
 					sayt:            false,
 					search:          false
 				}
 			}
 		};
 		searchEvent.search.origin[params.origin] = true;
 		if ('metadata' in params) {
 			searchEvent['metadata'] = params.metadata;
 		}
 		gbTracker.sendAutoSearchEvent(searchEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerAddToCartEvent(params) {
 		var addToCartEvent = {
 			cart: params
 		};
 		//console.log(addToCartEvent);
 		gbTracker.sendAddToCartEvent(addToCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerViewCartEvent(params) {
 		var viewCartEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.CartID,
 				items: params.Items
 			}
 		};
 //		console.log(viewCartEvent);
 		gbTracker.sendViewCartEvent(viewCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerRemoveFromCartEvent(params) {
 		var removeFromCartEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.CartID,
 				items: params.Items
 			}
 		};
 //		console.log(removeFromCartEvent);
 //		return;
 		gbTracker.sendRemoveFromCartEvent(removeFromCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerViewProductEvent(params) {
 		var viewProductEvent = {
 			product: params.product
 		};
 //		console.log(viewProductEvent);
 //		return;
 		gbTracker.sendViewProductEvent(viewProductEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerOrderEvent(params) {
 		var orderEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.cartId,
 				totalItems: params.totalItems,
 				totalQuantity: params.totalQuantity,
 				totalPrice: params.totalPrice,
 				items: params.items
 			}
 		};
 		gbTracker.sendOrderEvent(orderEvent);
 	}
 
 
 	// initialise the gbTracker if not initialiased yet
 	function initializeGbTracker(gbTrackerObject) {
 		if (gbTrackerObject !== null) {
 			return gbTrackerObject;
 		}
 		var gbTrackerLocal = new GbTracker('threebscientific', 'GermanyGerman');
 		
 			gbTrackerLocal.autoSetVisitor();
 		
 		return gbTrackerLocal;
 	}
   </script>

 	$(function() {
 		
 		$(".ga-click-tracking").on("click", function(e){
 			var eventCategory="unknown",eventAction="unknown",eventLabel="unknown",eventValue="unknown";
 			if ($(this).hasClass("ga-click-tracking")) {
 				eventAction = 'click';
 			}
 			eventCategory = $(this).data("ga-category");
 			eventLabel = $(this).data("ga-label");
 			eventValue = $(this).data("ga-value");
 			sendEventToGA(eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue);
 		});
 		$(".link-element[data-href]").on("click",function(e){
 			e.stopPropagation();
 			if ($(this).data("href") !== undefined) {
 				if ($(this).data("event-name") !== undefined && $(this).data("event-category") !== undefined) {
 					sendEventToGA($(this).data('event-category'),'click',$(this).data('event-name'),1);
 				}
 				window.location.href=$(this).data("href");
 			}
 		});
 	});
 
 	function sendEventToGA(eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue) {
 		if (eventValue===undefined) {
 			eventValue=1;
 		};
 		
 		ga('send','event',eventCategory,eventAction,eventLabel,eventValue);
 	};

 var addToCartAnimsCount = 0;

 		$('#SearchText').sayt({
 			subdomain: 'threebscientific',
 			collection: 'DEDE',
 			defaultImage: '',
 			area: 'GermanyGerman',
 			selectSearchTerm: function (data) {
 				$('#SearchText').val(data.value);
 				$('#SearchOrigin').val('sayt');
 				$('#SearchForm').submit();
 			},
 	        selectProduct: function (data) {
 				window.location.href = data.url;

 	        ,
 	        autocompleteTemplate: 'at',
 	        productTemplate: 'pt_DEDE',

 		$(".headerCart").popover({

 			html: true,
 			title: '<a href="https://www.3bscientific.de/cart.html">In Ihrem Warenkorb</a>',
 			content: function() {
 				return ShoppingCartSummaryContent;
 			},
 			placement: 'bottom'
 		});
 		$(".headerCart").on("mouseenter",function (e){
 			e.preventDefault();
 			e.stopPropagation();
 			if (ShoppingCartSummaryContent != null) {
 				$(".headerCart").popover('show');
 				
 					if (typeof viewShoppingCartSummaryEvent == 'function') {
 						viewShoppingCartSummaryEvent();
 					}
 				
 				var PopoverTop = parseInt($(".headerCart").next("div.popover:visible").css("top"));
 				$(".headerCart").next("div.popover:visible").css("top",(PopoverTop + 15).toString() + "px" );
 				$("#ShoppingCartSummary").closest(".popover").on("mouseleave", function(e){
 					e.preventDefault();
 					e.stopPropagation();
 					$("#ShoppingCartSummary").closest(".popover").unbind("mouseleave");
 					$(".headerCart").popover('hide');
 				});
 			} else {
 				$.post(
 					"/index.cfm?fuseaction=Cart.displayCartSummary"
 				).done( function (data){
 					ShoppingCartSummaryContent = data;
 					$(".headerCart").trigger('mouseenter');
 				});
 			}
 		});
 	
 	
 	$('.add-to-cart').on('click', function (e) {
 		e.preventDefault();
 		e.stopPropagation();
 		cartItemCount = null;
 		var imgtodrag = null;
 		ShoppingCartSummaryContent = null;
 		// submit the form as first in the background
 		$(this).closest('.AddProductToCartForm').submit();
 		// find the image to drag into the shopping cart
 		
 		if (imgtodrag == null || imgtodrag.length == 0) {
 			if ($('#ProductImageContainer').length > 0) {
 				imgtodrag = $('#ProductImageContainer').find("#ZoomerOuter").eq(0).find("img").eq(0);
 				if (imgtodrag.length === 0) {
 					imgtodrag = $('#ProductImageContainer').find("img");
 				}
 			} else {
 				var productID = $(this).closest('.AddProductToCartForm').find('[name=ProductID]').val();
 				imgtodrag = $('#productImage' + productID);
 			}
 		}
 		$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 'fast');
 
 		var cart = $('.shopping-cart');
 		if (imgtodrag.length > 0 && cart.length > 0) {
 			addToCartAnimsCount += 1;
 			var imgclone = imgtodrag.clone()
 				.offset({
 					top: imgtodrag.offset().top,
 					left: imgtodrag.offset().left
 				})
 				.css({
 					'opacity': '0.5',
 					'position': 'absolute',
 					'z-index': '100'
 	            })
 					.appendTo($('body'))
 					.animate({
 					'top': cart.offset().top + 10,
 					'left': cart.offset().left + 10,
 					'width': 75,
 					'height': 75
 	            }, 1500, 'easeInOutExpo');
 			imgclone.animate({
 					'width': 0,
 					'height': 0
 			}, function () {
 				$(this).detach();
 				addToCartAnimsCount -= 1;
 				if (cartItemCount != null && addToCartAnimsCount < 1) {
 					$(".CartItemCount").html(cartItemCount);
 					cartItemCount = null;
 				}
 			});
 		}
 	});
 
 });
 
 
 function loginDialog(displayMessage)
 {
 	var displayMessageParam = '';
 	if (displayMessage !== undefined) {
 		displayMessageParam = '&displayMessage=' + displayMessage;
 	}
 	$.post(
 		"https://www.3bscientific.de/index.cfm?fuseaction=Account.displayLoginPopup" + displayMessageParam
 	).done(function( data ) {
 		$('#LoginModalContainer .modal-body').html(data);
 		$('#LoginModalContainer .modal-footer #FormSubmit').show();
 		$('#LoginFormModal').modal('show');
 	});
 	return false;
 }
 
 function quickshopDialog()
 {
 	$.post(
 		"/index.cfm?fuseaction=Cart.displayQuickShop"
 	).done(function( data ) {
 		$('#QuickshopModalContainer .modal-body').html(data);
 		$('#QuickModalContainer .modal-footer #FormSubmit').show();
 		$('#QuickshopFormModal').modal('show');
 	});
 	return false;
 }
 
 
 	function getSearchURL(SearchText, SearchOrigin) {
 		var url = '/';
 		if (SearchText.length === 0) {
 			SearchText = ' ';
 		}
 		var SearchTextCleaned = SearchText.replace(/\//g,'--');
 		url += SearchTextCleaned.replace(/ /g,'+') + '/q/?SearchText=' + encodeURIComponent(SearchText);
 		if (SearchOrigin.length > 0) {
 			url += '&SearchOrigin=' + SearchOrigin;
 		}
 		return url;
 	}

    var TwitterStylesIntervalID;
 var TwitterStylesTries = 10;
 
 function setTwitterStyles() {
 	if ($("iframe#twitter-widget-0").contents().find('head').length > 0 || TwitterStylesTries < 1) {
 		$("iframe#twitter-widget-0").contents().find('head').append('<style>img.u-photo,img.avatar{display:none;}body{color:#58595b;font-family:"proxima-nova",sans-serif;}.header{padding-left:0!important;min-height:20px!important;}span.full-name{float:left;}span.p-name{color:#4a96fe!important;font-size:140%!important;font-weight:400!important;margin-right:5px;}span.p-nickname{color:#959595;}p.e-entry-title{font-size:14px!important;line-height:1.25em!important;}.tweet{padding-left:0!important}</style>');
 		clearInterval(TwitterStylesIntervalID);
 		return;
 	}
 	TwitterStylesTries--;
 }
 
 
 $(document).ready(function()
 {
 	$(".teaserSlider .slide").show();
 	$('.teaserSlider').bxSlider({
 		minSlides: 1,
 		maxSlides: 1,
 		auto: true,
 		speed: 1300,
 		pause: 5500,
 		controls: false
 	});
 	$("#EmailSignUpImage").click(function() {
 	  	$("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: $(document).height() }, "slow");
 	  	return false;
 	});
 	
 		
 		TwitterStylesIntervalID = setInterval(setTwitterStyles,1000);
 	
 });

   <script src="//cdn.groupbycloud.com/dist/gb-tracker-client-3.min.js">
   </script>
   <script type="text/javascript">
    var gbTracker = null;
 	$(document).ready(function() {
 		gbTracker = initializeGbTracker(gbTracker);
 	});
 
 	function sendGbTrackerEvent(eventName,params) {
 		gbTracker = initializeGbTracker(gbTracker);
 		switch(eventName) {
 			case 'search':
 				sendGbTrackerSearchEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'addToCart':
 				sendGbTrackerAddToCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'viewCart':
 				sendGbTrackerViewCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'removeFromCart':
 				sendGbTrackerRemoveFromCartEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'viewProduct':
 				sendGbTrackerViewProductEvent(params);
 				break;
 			case 'order':
 				sendGbTrackerOrderEvent(params);
 				break;
 		    default:
 				alert('unknown event');
 		}
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerSearchEvent(params) {
 		var searchEvent = {
 			search: {
 				id: params.id,
 				origin: {
 					recommendations: false,
 					navigation:      false,
 					dym:             false,
 					sayt:            false,
 					search:          false
 				}
 			}
 		};
 		searchEvent.search.origin[params.origin] = true;
 		if ('metadata' in params) {
 			searchEvent['metadata'] = params.metadata;
 		}
 		gbTracker.sendAutoSearchEvent(searchEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerAddToCartEvent(params) {
 		var addToCartEvent = {
 			cart: params
 		};
 		//console.log(addToCartEvent);
 		gbTracker.sendAddToCartEvent(addToCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerViewCartEvent(params) {
 		var viewCartEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.CartID,
 				items: params.Items
 			}
 		};
 //		console.log(viewCartEvent);
 		gbTracker.sendViewCartEvent(viewCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerRemoveFromCartEvent(params) {
 		var removeFromCartEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.CartID,
 				items: params.Items
 			}
 		};
 //		console.log(removeFromCartEvent);
 //		return;
 		gbTracker.sendRemoveFromCartEvent(removeFromCartEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerViewProductEvent(params) {
 		var viewProductEvent = {
 			product: params.product
 		};
 //		console.log(viewProductEvent);
 //		return;
 		gbTracker.sendViewProductEvent(viewProductEvent);
 	}
 
 	function sendGbTrackerOrderEvent(params) {
 		var orderEvent = {
 			cart: {
 				id: params.cartId,
 				totalItems: params.totalItems,
 				totalQuantity: params.totalQuantity,
 				totalPrice: params.totalPrice,
 				items: params.items
 			}
 		};
 		gbTracker.sendOrderEvent(orderEvent);
 	}
 
 
 	// initialise the gbTracker if not initialiased yet
 	function initializeGbTracker(gbTrackerObject) {
 		if (gbTrackerObject !== null) {
 			return gbTrackerObject;
 		}
 		var gbTrackerLocal = new GbTracker('threebscientific', 'GermanyGerman');
 		
 			gbTrackerLocal.autoSetVisitor();
 		
 		return gbTrackerLocal;
 	}
   </script>
